content

::: title
### [Beques d'Amazon dirigides a dones per a la innovació 2024-2025](/en/noticies/beques-damazon-dirigides-dones-la-innovacio-2024-2025 "Beques d’Amazon dirigides a dones per a la innovació 2024-2025")
:::

:::::: post_desc
::::: {.field .field-name-body .field-type-text-with-summary .field-label-hidden}
:::: field-items
::: {.field-item .even}

d'electrònica, telecomunicació o informàtica que compleixi amb els
requisits demanats.

::: title
### [InLab FIB collaboration with SEAT and Volkswagen Group Innovation](/en/news/inlab-fib-collaboration-seat-and-volkswagen-group-innovation "InLab FIB collaboration with SEAT and Volkswagen Group Innovation")
:::

:::::: post_desc

:::: field-items
::: {.field-item .even}

::: title
### [Antwerp Summer University Going Digital](/en/news/antwerp-summer-university-going-digital "Antwerp Summer University Going Digital")
:::

:::::: post_desc
::::: {.field .field-name-body .field-type-text-with-summary .field-label-hidden}
:::: field-items
::: {.field-item .even}
Interested in an online adventure along with like-minded people from all
over the world? Make your stay at home a little more educational and
join one of the seven exciting online courses offered!

::: title
### [Summer Academy 2020](/en/news/summer-academy-2020 "Summer Academy 2020")
:::

:::::: post_desc
::::: {.field .field-name-body .field-type-text-with-summary .field-label-hidden}
:::: field-items
::: {.field-item .even}
A four-week credit-bearing programme in Linköping,  Sweden --
Scandinavia, only available for students from LiU's partner
universities. No tuition fees! 
:::
::::
:::::

::: title
### [#bitsxlaMarató, the Hackathon that fights rare diseases](/en/news/bitsxlamarato-hackathon-fights-rare-diseases "#bitsxlaMarató, the Hackathon that fights rare diseases")
:::

:::::: post_desc
::::: {.field .field-name-body .field-type-text-with-summary .field-label-hidden}
:::: field-items
::: {.field-item .even}
Here comes the hackaton of solidarity, technology and health! \
This is the hackaton that collaborates with "la Marató de TV3", a
charity program organised every year at Christmas time by the public
television in Catalunya.\
This is the hackaton that will bring us positive energy and donations
for a good cause!!!

::: title
### [Do your TFM/TFG at Université de Lorraine next spring!!](/en/news/do-your-tfmtfg-universite-de-lorraine-next-spring "Do your TFM/TFG at Université de Lorraine next spring!!")
:::

:::::: post_desc
::::: {.field .field-name-body .field-type-text-with-summary .field-label-hidden}
:::: field-items
::: {.field-item .even}
If you are a MIRI, MAI, MEI or GEI student then you can apply to a
project in the IT area for the spring semester of the 2019-2020 academic
year.
:::
::::
:::::
::::::
::::::::::::
